`fitratio`: Get the maximum number of a ratio of units that will fit in specified (optional) capacity.
Arguments
`fitratio [materialCountListStr...]`

Optional last two arguments specifying capacity
 `100t 100m`

## AGP Information
**Updated:** 20-Jun-24 01:14 PM
### What is AGP?
* AGP stands for "Antares Grant Program" and exists to provide 750k AIC grants to less developed Antares-based players. (this includes those who are looking to move/expand into Antares)
 * We use the term "grant" to simply mean free money; you are not obligated to pay any of it back.
### Who is operating this program?
* The official project lead is currently @jvaler, however the other contributors operate somewhat autonomously. Determining who pays out grants is currently done randomly based on whoever volunteers first, which isn't ideal but ü§∑‚Äç‚ôÄÔ∏è
 * Said contributors are: @jvaler, @sidepipe, and @archielvahr
### What should I do with the money?
* placeholder
### How can I join?
* placeholder
